An attempt to reconcile Hooker's synonymy and Lushington's synonyms and English equivalents produces inconsistencies. Lushington gives 'emetic nut' as the English equivalent, with qualifiers of several species:Lamk. =Wall. 'common emetic nut' ~ marukkārai, 1475>: Lamk. =Schlecht. 'bedaly e. n.' ~ 1475>: 'grey e.n.'. But Hooker's further synonymy withLamk. ofWilld. disagrees with Lushington'sLamk. =Willd. 'honey-thorn'. To be noted also is Hooker'sRoxb. =Wall., and Lushington's'spinous honey-thorn'. Our dictionaries in part defy exact interpretation by species. DED 1234 ~
